\mbox{\Hypertarget{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_builder_a1fcfad731fc317b44b310aa8b89c9953}\label{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_builder_a1fcfad731fc317b44b310aa8b89c9953}} 
\index{okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder@{okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder}!notParentedToCurrentTask@{notParentedToCurrentTask}}
\index{notParentedToCurrentTask@{notParentedToCurrentTask}!okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder@{okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{notParentedToCurrentTask()}{notParentedToCurrentTask()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_builder}{Chassis\+Controller\+Builder}} \& okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Controller\+Builder\+::not\+Parented\+To\+Current\+Task (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Prevents parenting the internal tasks started by this builder to the current task, meaning they will not be deleted once the current task is deleted. This can cause runaway tasks, but is sometimes the desired behavior (e.\+x., if you want to use this builder once in {\ttfamily autonomous} and then again in {\ttfamily opcontrol}).

Read more about this in the \mbox{[}builders and tasks tutorial\mbox{]} (docs/tutorials/concepts/builders-\/and-\/tasks.\+md).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An ongoing builder. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder@{okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder}!parentedToCurrentTask@{parentedToCurrentTask}}
\index{parentedToCurrentTask@{parentedToCurrentTask}!okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder@{okapi::ChassisControllerBuilder}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parentedToCurrentTask()}{parentedToCurrentTask()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_builder}{Chassis\+Controller\+Builder}} \& okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Controller\+Builder\+::parented\+To\+Current\+Task (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Parents the internal tasks started by this builder to the current task, meaning they will be deleted once the current task is deleted. The {\ttfamily initialize} and {\ttfamily competition\+\_\+initialize} tasks are never parented to. This is the default behavior.

Read more about this in the \mbox{[}builders and tasks tutorial\mbox{]} (docs/tutorials/concepts/builders-\/and-\/tasks.\+md).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An ongoing builder. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Sets the \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_time_util_factory}{Time\+Util\+Factory}} used when building a \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller}{Chassis\+Controller}}. This instance will be given to the \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller}{Chassis\+Controller}} (not to controllers it uses). The default is the static \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_time_util_factory}{Time\+Util\+Factory}}.
